45	@Override


46	public Authentication extractAuthentication(Map<String, ?> map) {


47		if (map.containsKey(USERNAME)) {


48			Collection<? extends GrantedAuthority> authorities = getAuthorities(map);


49


50			String username = (String) map.get(USERNAME);


51			String id = String.valueOf(map.get(SecurityEnum.DETAILS_USER_ID));


52			String organId = String.valueOf(map.get(SecurityEnum.DETAILS_ORGAN_ID));


53			String tenantId = String.valueOf(map.get(SecurityEnum.DETAILS_TENANT_ID));



53			BizUser user = new BizUser(id, organId, tenantId, username, N_A, true


54					, true, true, true, authorities);


55			return new UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken(user, N_A, authorities);


56		}


57		return null;


58	}


59


60	private Collection<? extends GrantedAuthority> getAuthorities(Map<String, ?> map) {



61		Object authorities = map.get(AUTHORITIES);


62		if (authorities instanceof String) {


63			return AuthorityUtils.commaSeparatedStringToAuthorityList((String) authorities);


64		}


65		if (authorities instanceof Collection) {


66			return AuthorityUtils.commaSeparatedStringToAuthorityList(StringUtils


67					.collectionToCommaDelimitedString((Collection<?>) authorities));


68		}


69		return new ArrayList<GrantedAuthority>();


70	}

158	private List<String> findKeysForPage(String patternKey, int pageNum, int pageSize) {


159		ScanOptions options = ScanOptions.scanOptions().match(patternKey).build();


160		RedisSerializer<String> redisSerializer = (RedisSerializer<String>) redisTemplate.getKeySerializer();


161		Cursor cursor = (Cursor) redisTemplate.executeWithStickyConnection(redisConnection -> new ConvertingCursor<>(redisConnection.scan(options), redisSerializer::deserialize));


162		List<String> result = new ArrayList<>();


163		int tmpIndex = 0;


164		int startIndex = (pageNum - 1) * pageSize;


165		int end = pageNum * pageSize;


166


167		assert cursor != null;

19		if(System.getProperty("os.name").toLowerCase().contains("win")){


20			uploadPath = "D:/uploads/";


21		}


22		// 上传的图片映射



22		registry.addResourceHandler("/uploads/**")


23				.addResourceLocations("file:" + uploadPath)


24				.setCachePeriod(0);


25


26		// 默认静态资源：static 文件夹


27//		registry.addResourceHandler("/**")


28//				.addResourceLocations("classpath:/static/");


29	}



30


31	@Bean


32	public WebServerFactoryCustomizer<ConfigurableServletWebServerFactory> enableDefaultServlet() {


33		return factory -> factory.setRegisterDefaultServlet(true);


34	}


35}

import feign.RequestInterceptor;
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.condition.ConditionalOnClass;
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.condition.ConditionalOnProperty;
import org.springframework.cloud.security.oauth2.client.AccessTokenContextRelay;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
import org.springframework.security.oauth2.client.OAuth2ClientContext;
import org.springframework.security.oauth2.client.resource.OAuth2ProtectedResourceDetails;

/**
* fegin 配置增强
*
* @author
*/
@Configuration
@ConditionalOnClass(Feign.class)
public class BaseFeignConfiguration {

@Bean
@ConditionalOnProperty(&quot;security.oauth2.client.client-id&quot;)
public RequestInterceptor oauth2FeignRequestInterceptor(OAuth2ClientContext oAuth2ClientContext,
OAuth2ProtectedResourceDetails resource,
AccessTokenContextRelay accessTokenContextRelay) {
return new BaseFeignClientInterceptor(oAuth2ClientContext, resource, accessTokenContextRelay);
}

}

[CRITICAL - 高危风险特殊处理]

- 反序列化漏洞
- SSRF/CSRF类漏洞

[CRITICAL - 拒绝阈值调整]

- No Assumption（禁止假设）
- Evidence Driven（基于代码事实）
- Deterministic Output（稳定输出）
- 优先反驳
- 攻击链默认不成立

[LANGUAGE REQUIREMENTS]
- 所有输出必须使用简体中文
- 专业术语保留英文（如 SQL Injection, XSS, CSRF, SSRF）
- 描述、结论必须用中文
- **攻击链名称（attack_chain_name）必须使用中文自然语言描述，禁止使用英文蛇形命名**

[DECISION RULES]
- 攻击路径完整可执行 → ACCEPT
- 攻击路径不完整但有可疑迹象 → ESCALATE（标记待人工复核）
- 仅理论可能无法实际验证 → UNCERTAIN
- 明确不可行或被防御完全阻断 → REFUTE
- 只能挑战CONFIRMED信号

[HARD RULES]
- 禁止输出解释性文本
- 禁止输出推理过程
- 禁止偏离任务
- 禁止补充未提供的信息
- 禁止使用&quot;可能/大概/推测&quot;等词
- 禁止推测
- 禁止补全逻辑
- 禁止编造攻击路径
- 所有结论必须来自输入
- 禁止空洞的&quot;Unknown&quot;输出

[STRICT OUTPUT CONTRACT]
verdict只能是：
- ACCEPT: 攻击链可行
- REFUTE: 攻击链不可行
- ESCALATE: 需要人工复核
- UNCERTAIN: 无法确定

必须包含challenged_signal_id指向上游攻击链。

[语言约束]
当前代码语言: Java
- 只验证 Java 语言的漏洞利用
- 禁止验证其他语言的漏洞利用

45	@Override


46	public Authentication extractAuthentication(Map<String, ?> map) {


47		if (map.containsKey(USERNAME)) {


48			Collection<? extends GrantedAuthority> authorities = getAuthorities(map);


49


50			String username = (String) map.get(USERNAME);


51			String id = String.valueOf(map.get(SecurityEnum.DETAILS_USER_ID));


52			String organId = String.valueOf(map.get(SecurityEnum.DETAILS_ORGAN_ID));


53			String tenantId = String.valueOf(map.get(SecurityEnum.DETAILS_TENANT_ID));



53			BizUser user = new BizUser(id, organId, tenantId, username, N_A, true


54					, true, true, true, authorities);


55			return new UsernamePasswordAuthenticationToken(user, N_A, authorities);


56		}


57		return null;


58	}


59


60	private Collection<? extends GrantedAuthority> getAuthorities(Map<String, ?> map) {



61		Object authorities = map.get(AUTHORITIES);


62		if (authorities instanceof String) {


63			return AuthorityUtils.commaSeparatedStringToAuthorityList((String) authorities);


64		}


65		if (authorities instanceof Collection) {


66			return AuthorityUtils.commaSeparatedStringToAuthorityList(StringUtils


67					.collectionToCommaDelimitedString((Collection<?>) authorities));


68		}


69		return new ArrayList<GrantedAuthority>();


70	}
证据链
  • 从map中获取AUTHORITIES对象，直接用于后续解析，缺少对token签名或来源的二次校验。 📍 C:\1AAA_PROJECT\HOS\HOS-LS\real-project\bizspring-open-main\bizspring-base\bizspring-base-security\src\main\java\cn\bizspring\cloud\common\security\component\BaseUserAuthenticationConverter.java:53
  • 如果authorities是String类型，直接调用AuthorityUtils.commaSeparatedStringToAuthorityList解析，可注入任意数组。 📍 C:\1AAA_PROJECT\HOS\HOS-LS\real-project\bizspring-open-main\bizspring-base\bizspring-base-security\src\main\java\cn\bizspring\cloud\common\security\component\BaseUserAuthenticationConverter.java:54
  • 如果authorities是Collection，则通过StringUtils.collectionToCommaDelimitedString转换为逗号分隔字符串后同样解析，存在相同风险。 📍 C:\1AAA_PROJECT\HOS\HOS-LS\real-project\bizspring-open-main\bizspring-base\bizspring-base-security\src\main\java\cn\bizspring\cloud\common\security\component\BaseUserAuthenticationConverter.java:56

142	@Inside


143	@PostMapping("/page")


144	public ResponseEntity<Page> tokenList(@RequestBody Map<String, Object> params) {


145		//根据分页参数获取对应数据


146		String key = String.format("%s*:%s", BASE_OAUTH_ACCESS, TenantContextHolder.getTenantId());


147		List<String> pages = findKeysForPage(key, MapUtil.getInt(params, PageEnum.CURRENT)


148				, MapUtil.getInt(params, PageEnum.SIZE));


149


150		redisTemplate.setKeySerializer(new StringRedisSerializer());



150		redisTemplate.setValueSerializer(new JdkSerializationRedisSerializer());


151		Page result = new Page(MapUtil.getInt(params, PageEnum.CURRENT), MapUtil.getInt(params, PageEnum.SIZE));


152		result.setRecords(redisTemplate.opsForValue().multiGet(pages));


153		result.setTotal(Long.valueOf(redisTemplate.keys(key).size()));


154		return R.ok(result);


155	}

157



158	private List<String> findKeysForPage(String patternKey, int pageNum, int pageSize) {


159		ScanOptions options = ScanOptions.scanOptions().match(patternKey).build();


160		RedisSerializer<String> redisSerializer = (RedisSerializer<String>) redisTemplate.getKeySerializer();


161		Cursor cursor = (Cursor) redisTemplate.executeWithStickyConnection(redisConnection -> new ConvertingCursor<>(redisConnection.scan(options), redisSerializer::deserialize));


162		List<String> result = new ArrayList<>();


163		int tmpIndex = 0;


164		int startIndex = (pageNum - 1) * pageSize;


165		int end = pageNum * pageSize;


166


167		assert cursor != null;
证据链
  • JdkSerializationRedisSerializer使用Java原生序列化，存在已知的安全风险 📍 C:\1AAA_PROJECT\HOS\HOS-LS\real-project\bizspring-open-main\bizspring-business\bizspring-auth\src\main\java\cn\bizspring\cloud\auth\controller\TokenController.java:150
